***непрерывный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:непрерывный.html>непреры́вный</a> (6222)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:непрерывный.html>непреры́вный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">neprerývnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>continuous, uninterrupted, unbroken</li>
<li>contiguous <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">connecting without a break</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>ongoing, continued, continual</li>
<li>sustained</li>
<li>incessant, ceaseless, unceasing, perpetual</li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

***неприкаянный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:неприкаянный.html>неприка́янный</a> (21286)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Has the form of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недопить.html>не-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ne-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">*прика́янный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">*prikájannyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, putative past passive participle of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">*прика́ять</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">*prikájatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; compare <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:каяться.html>ка́яться</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kájatʹsja</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to repent</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:окаянный.html>окая́нный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">okajánnyj</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">damned, cursed</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:неприкаянный.html>неприка́янный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">neprikájannyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)неприка́яннее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)неприка́янней</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> restless, not knowing what to do</li>
<li>unsettled, homeless</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:неприкосновенный.html>неприкоснове́нный</a> (21711)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:неприкосновенный.html>неприкоснове́нный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">neprikosnovénnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>untouchable, inviolable, immune, sacrosanct</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> reserve
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:неприкосновенный.html>неприкоснове́нный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:запас.html>запа́с</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>neprikosnovénnyj</b> zapás</i> ― <span class="e-translation">reserve supply</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>The term is not to be confused with <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">неприкаса́емый</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">neprikasájemyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.</li></ul>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:при.html>при</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:коса.html>кос</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:но.html>но</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:вена.html>ве́н</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ный</b>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:непримиримость.html>непримири́мость</a> (26241)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:непримиримость.html>непримири́мость</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">neprimirímostʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:непримиримость.html>непримири́мости</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:непримиримость.html>непримири́мости</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:непримиримость.html>непримири́мостей</a></b>)

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недопить.html>не-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ne-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:примирить.html>примири́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">primirítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-и́мый</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ímyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:непримиримый.html>непримири́мый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">neprimirímyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>irreconcilable, unappeasable, implacable
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:непримиримый.html>непримири́мая</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:борьба.html>борьба́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>neprimirímaja</b> borʹbá</i> ― <span class="e-translation">uncompromising struggle; war to the knife</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вести.html>вести</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:непримиримый.html>непримири́мую</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:борьба.html>борьбу́</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:против.html>про́тив</a>)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">vesti <b>neprimirímuju</b> borʹbú (prótiv)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to wage a relentless struggle (against)</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>incompatible, irreconcilable
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:непримиримый.html>непримири́мые</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:противоречие.html>противоре́чия</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>neprimirímyje</b> protivoréčija</i> ― <span class="e-translation">irreconcilable contradictions</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недопить.html>не-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ne-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:принуждённый.html>принуждённый</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">prinuždjónnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

</p>
<ol><li>unconstrained</li>
<li>informal</li>
<li>unforced, unstrained</li>
<li>at ease <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">free of anxiety</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>easy, free, natural, casual (speech, manners, etc.)</li>
<li>spontaneous, unstudied</li>
<li>unrestrained</li>
<li>unaffected</li>
<li>cavalier</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:неприязнь.html>неприя́знь</a> (6659)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:неприязнь.html>неприя́знь</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">neprijáznʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:неприязнь.html>неприя́зни</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:неприязнь.html>неприя́зни</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:неприязнь.html>неприя́зней</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>enmity, hostility <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">hostile or unfriendly disposition</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>

<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:про.html>про</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:из.html>из</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:воля.html>во́ль</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ный</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:прилагательное.html>Прилага́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:качественный.html>ка́чественное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 1*a. <a href = vnd.unilang:сравнительный.html>Сравни́тельная</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:степень.html>сте́пень</a> — <i>непроизвольнее.</i>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:приставка.html>Приста́вка</a>: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:недопить.html>не-</a></b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>ко́рень</a>: <b>-произволь-</b>; суффикс: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:порядочный.html>-н</a></b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ый</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.
</p>
